In `sg-benchmarks/kubernetes-client-go`, the typed Deployment client is implemented in `gentype/type.go`. The `Client[T].Create()` method (line 244) constructs and sends the HTTP request:\\n\\n```go\\nfunc (c *Client[T]) Create(ctx context.Context, obj T, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (T, error) {\\n    result := c.newObject()\\n    err := c.client.Post().\\n        UseProtobufAsDefaultIfPreferred(c.prefersProtobuf).\\n        NamespaceIfScoped(c.namespace, c.namespace != \\\"\\\").\\n        Resource(c.resource).\\n        VersionedParams(&opts, c.parameterCodec).\\n        Body(obj).\\n        Do(ctx).\\n        Into(result)\\n    return result, err\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThis method:\\n1. In `kubernetes/kubernetes`, Deployments are handled by the `REST` type defined in `pkg/registry/apps/deployment/storage/storage.go` (line 88-90):\\n\\n```go\\ntype REST struct {\\n    *genericregistry.Store\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThe `REST` handler is created by `NewREST()` (line 93), which initializes a `genericregistry.Store` with Deployment-specific strategies:\\n\\n```go\\nstore := &genericregistry.Store{\\n    NewFunc: func() runtime.Object { return &apps.Deployment{} },\\n    NewListFunc: func() runtime.Object { return &apps.DeploymentList{} },\\n    DefaultQualifiedResource: apps.Resource(\\\"deployments\\\"),\\n    CreateStrategy: deployment.Strategy,\\n    UpdateStrategy: deployment.Strategy,\\n    DeleteStrategy: deployment.Strategy,\\n    // ...\\n}\\n```\\n\\nWhen the REST handler processes the create request, it delegates to the `Store.Create()` method from `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/generic/registry/store.go` (line 446). Invokes admission control plugins to allow or reject the Deployment\\n3. Calls validation via `createValidation` callback (which uses `appsvalidation.ValidateDeployment()`)\\n4. Persists the object via `e.Storage.Create()` to the etcd backend\\n5. Returns HTTP 201 Created to the client\\n\\nThe `CreateStrategy` (deployed.Strategy) implements validation rules specific to Deployments, such as validating replica counts, selector label matching, and pod template specifications.\\n\\n### Layer 3: Storage Backend (etcd)\\n\\nThe `Store.Create()` method calls `e.Storage.Create()`, which routes to the etcd3 storage backend in `kubernetes/kubernetes` at `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storage/etcd3/store.go`. The etcd3 `store.Create()` method (line 241) translates the generic storage interface:\\n\\n1. Encodes the Deployment object using the appropriate codec (protobuf or JSON)\\n2. In `etcd-io/etcd`, the `storeTxnWrite.Put()` method at `server/mvcc/kvstore_txn.go` (line 109) is the entry point:\\n\\n```go\\nfunc (tw *storeTxnWrite) Put(key, value []byte, lease lease.LeaseID) int64 {\\n    tw.put(key, value, lease)\\n    return tw.beginRev + 1\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThe internal `put()` method (line 190) performs the critical steps:\\n\\n1. Generates a unique revision number for this write\\n2. Checks if the key previously existed (for update vs. insert semantics)\\n3. Marshals the Deployment into an `mvccpb.KeyValue` protobuf:\\n   ```go\\n   kv := mvccpb.KeyValue{\\n       Key: key,\\n       Value: value,\\n       CreateRevision: c,\\n       ModRevision: rev,\\n       Version: ver,\\n       Lease: int64(leaseID),\\n   }\\n   d, err := kv.Marshal()\\n   ```\\n4. This persists the Deployment to disk across the etcd cluster.\\n\\n### Complete Request Path\\n\\n```\\nClient Application\\n    ↓\\nkubernetes-client-go: gentype/type.go:244 - Client.Create()\\n    ↓ (HTTP POST)\\nKubernetes API Server\\n    ↓\\nkubernetes/kubernetes: pkg/registry/apps/deployment/storage/storage.go:88 - REST handler\\n    ↓\\nkubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/generic/registry/store.go:446 - Store.Create()\\n    ↓\\nkubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storage/etcd3/store.go:241 - store.Create()\\n    ↓\\netcd-io/etcd: server/mvcc/kvstore_txn.go:109 - storeTxnWrite.Put()\\n    ↓\\netcd-io/etcd: server/mvcc/backend/batch_tx.go:145 - batchTx.UnsafeSeqPut()\\n    ↓\\nBoltDB (Disk Persistence)\\n    ↓\\nHTTP Response 201 Created\\n    ↓\\nClient Application receives Deployment object\\n```\\n\\n### Key Design Insights\\n\\n1. **Separation of Concerns**: The client library knows nothing about REST endpoints—it uses a generic REST client interface. The API server knows nothing about etcd internals—it uses an abstract storage interface. This enables swapping implementations.\\n\\n2. **Strategy Pattern**: The `CreateStrategy` allows per-resource-type customization of validation and preparation without modifying core API server code.\\n\\n3. **MVCC Semantics**: etcd tracks multiple versions of each key, enabling watch-based updates and atomic compare-and-swap operations that Kubernetes relies on for coordination.\\n\\n4. **Revision Tracking**: Every Deployment creation increments etcd's revision counter, enabling clients to detect changes and synchronize cluster state.\\n\\n5. **Index Maintenance**: etcd's in-memory kvindex allows efficient key lookups without scanning the entire backend store on every read.\\n\\nThis architecture demonstrates Kubernetes' commitment to clean layering—each component has a well-defined responsibility, and changes flow predictably through the system from client to durable storage.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":559,"cache_read_input_tokens":41879,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":559},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1befcfce-f39b-45fc-8907-c10a5f633c71","uuid":"55ebafdd-e408-43d7-801e-800c57eae3f7"}

Returns HTTP 201 Created to the client\\n\\nThe `CreateStrategy` (deployed.Strategy) implements validation rules specific to Deployments, such as validating replica counts, selector label matching, and pod template specifications.\\n\\n### Layer 3: Storage Backend (etcd)\\n\\nThe `Store.Create()` method calls `e.Storage.Create()`, which routes to the etcd3 storage backend in `kubernetes/kubernetes` at `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storage/etcd3/store.go`. The etcd3 `store.Create()` method (line 241) translates the generic storage interface:\\n\\n1. Encodes the Deployment object using the appropriate codec (protobuf or JSON)\\n2. Calls `s.client.Kubernetes.OptimisticPut()` to initiate the etcd write\\n3. Handles conflict resolution and revision tracking for MVCC (Multi-Version Concurrency Control)\\n\\nThis delegates to the etcd distributed key-value store. In `etcd-io/etcd`, the `storeTxnWrite.Put()` method at `server/mvcc/kvstore_txn.go` (line 109) is the entry point:\\n\\n```go\\nfunc (tw *storeTxnWrite) Put(key, value []byte, lease lease.LeaseID) int64 {\\n    tw.put(key, value, lease)\\n    return tw.beginRev + 1\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThe internal `put()` method (line 190) performs the critical steps:\\n\\n1. Generates a unique revision number for this write\\n2. Checks if the key previously existed (for update vs. insert semantics)\\n3. Marshals the Deployment into an `mvccpb.KeyValue` protobuf:\\n   ```go\\n   kv := mvccpb.KeyValue{\\n       Key: key,\\n       Value: value,\\n       CreateRevision: c,\\n       ModRevision: rev,\\n       Version: ver,\\n       Lease: int64(leaseID),\\n   }\\n   d, err := kv.Marshal()\\n   ```\\n4. Calls `tw.tx.UnsafeSeqPut(buckets.Key, ibytes, d)` at line 226 to write the marshaled data\\n5. Updates the in-memory index with `tw.s.kvindex.Put()` for fast future lookups\\n6. Records the change in `tw.changes` for transaction tracking\\n\\nFinally, the backend transaction's `UnsafeSeqPut()` method in `server/mvcc/backend/batch_tx.go` (line 145) executes the write to the underlying BoltDB store via `bucket.Put(key, value)`. This persists the Deployment to disk across the etcd cluster.\\n\\n### Complete Request Path\\n\\n```\\nClient Application\\n    ↓\\nkubernetes-client-go: gentype/type.go:244 - Client.Create()\\n    ↓ (HTTP POST)\\nKubernetes API Server\\n    ↓\\nkubernetes/kubernetes: pkg/registry/apps/deployment/storage/storage.go:88 - REST handler\\n    ↓\\nkubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/generic/registry/store.go:446 - Store.Create()\\n    ↓\\nkubernetes/kubernetes: staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storage/etcd3/store.go:241 - store.Create()\\n    ↓\\netcd-io/etcd: server/mvcc/kvstore_txn.go:109 - storeTxnWrite.Put()\\n    ↓\\netcd-io/etcd: server/mvcc/backend/batch_tx.go:145 - batchTx.UnsafeSeqPut()\\n    ↓\\nBoltDB (Disk Persistence)\\n    ↓\\nHTTP Response 201 Created\\n    ↓\\nClient Application receives Deployment object\\n```\\n\\n### Key Design Insights\\n\\n1. **Separation of Concerns**: The client library knows nothing about REST endpoints—it uses a generic REST client interface. The API server knows nothing about etcd internals—it uses an abstract storage interface. This enables swapping implementations.\\n\\n2. **Strategy Pattern**: The `CreateStrategy` allows per-resource-type customization of validation and preparation without modifying core API server code.\\n\\n3. **MVCC Semantics**: etcd tracks multiple versions of each key, enabling watch-based updates and atomic compare-and-swap operations that Kubernetes relies on for coordination.\\n\\n4. **Revision Tracking**: Every Deployment creation increments etcd's revision counter, enabling clients to detect changes and synchronize cluster state.\\n\\n5. **Index Maintenance**: etcd's in-memory kvindex allows efficient key lookups without scanning the entire backend store on every read.\\n\\nThis architecture demonstrates Kubernetes' commitment to clean layering—each component has a well-defined responsibility, and changes flow predictably through the system from client to durable storage.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
